<section id="index-vouchers" class="index-vouchers">
	<div class="container">

		<div class="voucher-list"></div>
		
		<div  id="btnNextList-voucher" style=" font-size: 14px; font-weight: bold; color: #990000; margin-top: 10px; text-decoration-line: underline; text-align: center; text-decoration-style: double; ">

<div class="voucher-detail-isshown"></div>

<script>
	window.indexVoucherId = 'TGSF15K,TGSFTL10PT,TGSF25K,TGSFSUN10K'.split(',').map(item => item.trim())
</script>
<script defer>
	function initDraggble(){
		let startPosition = 0;
		let draggedDown = false;
		let distance = 0
		$(function() {
			let startPosition = 0;
			let distance = 0;
			let draggedDown = false;

			$('.coupon-detail-container').draggable({
				//handle: '.handle',
				axis: 'y',
				revert: function() {
					return !draggedDown;
				},
				start: function(event, ui) {
					startPosition = ui.position.top;
				},
				drag: function(event, ui) {
					distance = ui.position.top - startPosition;
					if (ui.position.top < -50) {
						ui.position.top = -50;
					}
					if (distance > 50 && distance <= 200) {
						draggedDown = true;
					} else if (distance > 200) {
						$(this).draggable('disable');
						// Close this element
						$('body').removeClass('show-voucher-detail');
						$('.coupon-item').removeClass('show-detail');
						$(this).draggable('enable');
					} else {
						draggedDown = false;
					}
				},
				stop: function(event, ui) {
					if (draggedDown) {
						$('body').removeClass('show-voucher-detail');
						$('.coupon-item').removeClass('show-detail');
						setTimeout(()=> $(this).css({ top: 0 }) , 200)
						//$(this).css({ top: 0 });
					} else {
						console.log('Dragged down but not enough to trigger action, reverting');
						$(this).animate({ top: 0 }, 200);
					}
				}
			}); 
		});
	}
	function getHrvVouchers(){
		$.ajax({
			url: '/promotions.json',
			type: 'POST',
			dataType: 'json',
			contentType: 'application/json',
			data: JSON.stringify({showonwebsite: true}),
			success: data => {
				renderHrvVouchers(data.promotions)
				if(window.screen.width < 768){
					initDraggble()
				}
			},
			error: function() {}
		});
	}
	function renderHrvVouchers(voucher_list){
		if(!voucher_list) return
		var filteredVouchers = voucher_list.filter(item=> window.indexVoucherId.includes(item.code) )
		var voucherListHtml = ''
		let savings,
				requirements,
				expire

		$.each(filteredVouchers, function(i, item) {
			savings = item.savings<= 100 ? item.savings + '%' : item.savings / 1000 + "K"
			requirements = item.order_over >= 1000? item.order_over / 1000 + "K": (item.order_over == 0? '0đ': item.order_over + ' sản phẩm')
			expire = item.enddate? dayjs(item.enddate).format('DD/MM/YYYY'): false
			voucherListHtml += `
				<div class="voucher-item coupon-item" data-id="hrv_p-${item.code}" data-code="${item.code}" data-req="${requirements}" data-sav="${savings}" data-exp=${expire}>
							<div class="item-ribbon">
								<div class="item-ribbon__left item-icon">
									<img src="https://theme.hstatic.net/1000006063/1001240910/14/logo.png" alt="voucher-icon">
	</div>
								<div class="item-ribbon__right item-info">
									<div class="item-info__upper">
										<div class="heading">
											<p class="title">Giảm ${savings}</p>
											<a href="javascript:void(0);" class="view-coupon-btn" data-container="body" data-toggle="popover" data-placement="bottom" data-content="#hrv_p-${item.code}"><span class="dt">Điều kiện</span><span class="mb">i</span></a>
	</div>
										<p class="condition">Đơn hàng từ ${requirements}</p>
										${item.max_amount_apply != null ? ` <p class="condition"> Giảm tối đa ${Haravan.formatMoney(item.max_amount_apply * 100,window.F1GEN_vars.formatMoney)}</p>`:``}
	${item.entitled_collections.length > 0 ? ` <p class="condition">Áp dụng cho nhóm <a href="${item.entitled_collections[0].url}" title="Nhóm ${item.entitled_collections[0].title}">${item.entitled_collections[0].title}</a></p>`:`<p class="condition">Áp dụng cho tất cả sản phẩm</p>`}
	</div>
									<div class="item-info__lower">
										<a href="${item.entitled_collections.length > 0 ? `${item.entitled_collections[0].url}`:`/collections/san-pham-ban-chay`}" class="save-voucher-btn use-coupon-btn">
										<span class="copy-txt">Lưu</span>
		<span class="coupon-ani">
	+1
	<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M4 4C2.89543 4 2 4.89543 2 6V10.5H3C3.82843 10.5 4.5 11.1716 4.5 12C4.5 12.8284 3.82843 13.5 3 13.5H2V18C2 19.1046 2.89543 20 4 20H9V18H10V20H20C21.1046 20 22 19.1046 22 18V13.5H20.5C19.6716 13.5 19 12.8284 19 12C19 11.1716 19.6716 10.5 20.5 10.5H22V6C22 4.89543 21.1046 4 20 4H10V6H9V4H4ZM10 7.5H9V9.5H10V7.5ZM9 11H10V13H9V11ZM10 14.5H9V16.5H10V14.5Z" fill="#ee4d2d"></path></svg>
	</span>
	</a>
										<span>${expire? 'HSD: ' + expire: ''}</span>

	</div>
	</div>
	</div>

												<div class="coupon-item__view-detail" id="hrv_p-${item.code}">
            <div class="coupon-detail-container">
                          <a href="javascript:void(0);" class="handle"></a>
													<div class="detail-code">
														<span>Mã</span>
														<span class="detail-code__code">${item.code}
															<a class="use-coupon-btn">
															<svg width="20" height="20" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 64 64"><g data-name="Layer 3"><path d="M40.63,13H12.38A4.69,4.69,0,0,0,7.7,17.67V57.31A4.69,4.69,0,0,0,12.38,62H40.63a4.69,4.69,0,0,0,4.69-4.69V17.67A4.69,4.69,0,0,0,40.63,13Zm2.69,44.33A2.69,2.69,0,0,1,40.63,60H12.38A2.69,2.69,0,0,1,9.7,57.31V17.67A2.69,2.69,0,0,1,12.38,15H40.63a2.69,2.69,0,0,1,2.69,2.69Z"/><path d="M51.74,2H23.26a4.58,4.58,0,0,0-4.58,4.57v3.55a1,1,0,0,0,2,0V6.57A2.58,2.58,0,0,1,23.26,4H51.74A2.57,2.57,0,0,1,54.3,6.57V46.44A2.58,2.58,0,0,1,51.74,49H48.5a1,1,0,0,0,0,2h3.24a4.58,4.58,0,0,0,4.57-4.58V6.57A4.57,4.57,0,0,0,51.74,2Z"/></g></svg>
	</a>
	</span>
	</div>
													<div class="detail-exp">
														<span>Hạn sử dụng</span>
														<span>${expire? expire: 'Không giới hạn'}</span>
	</div>

													<div class="detail-details">
    												<ul class="details">
     							 				 		<li class="detail">Giảm ngay ${savings}</li>
      												<li class="detail">Cho đơn tối thiểu ${requirements}</li>
${item.entitled_collections.length > 0 ? ` <li class="detail">Áp dụng cho nhóm <a href="${item.entitled_collections[0].url}" title="Nhóm ${item.entitled_collections[0].title}">${item.entitled_collections[0].title}</a></li>`:``}
	</ul>
	</div>
													<div class="detail-action"><a href="${item.entitled_collections.length > 0 ? `${item.entitled_collections[0].url}`:`/collections/san-pham-ban-chay`}" class="save-voucher-btn use-coupon-btn">
																							<span class="copy-txt">Lưu</span>
		<span class="coupon-ani">
	+1
	<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M4 4C2.89543 4 2 4.89543 2 6V10.5H3C3.82843 10.5 4.5 11.1716 4.5 12C4.5 12.8284 3.82843 13.5 3 13.5H2V18C2 19.1046 2.89543 20 4 20H9V18H10V20H20C21.1046 20 22 19.1046 22 18V13.5H20.5C19.6716 13.5 19 12.8284 19 12C19 11.1716 19.6716 10.5 20.5 10.5H22V6C22 4.89543 21.1046 4 20 4H10V6H9V4H4ZM10 7.5H9V9.5H10V7.5ZM9 11H10V13H9V11ZM10 14.5H9V16.5H10V14.5Z" fill="#ee4d2d"></path></svg>
	</span>

	</a></div>
    											<span class="close-detail-btn"></span>
	</div>
	</div>

	</div>`;
		})
		$('#index-vouchers .voucher-list').html(voucherListHtml)
	}
	var first_load = true;
	document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
		if(!first_load) return
		getHrvVouchers()
		if (window.screen.width < 767) {
			$('body').removeClass('show-voucher-detail');
			$('.coupon-item').removeClass('show-detail');
			$(document).on('click', '.coupon-item .view-coupon-btn', function(e) {
				e.stopPropagation();
				$(this).parents('.coupon-item').addClass('show-detail')
				$('body').addClass('show-voucher-detail')
			})
			$(document).on('click', 'body', function(e) {
				const closeFlag = e.target.classList.contains('voucher-detail-isshown')
				if (! closeFlag) return
				$('body').removeClass('show-voucher-detail');
				$('.coupon-item').removeClass('show-detail');
			})
		}
		else {
			$(document).on('mouseenter', '.coupon-item .view-coupon-btn', function() {
				$('.coupon-item').removeClass('show-detail')
				$(this).parents('.coupon-item').addClass('show-detail')
			})
			$(document).on('mouseleave', '.coupon-item__view-detail', function() {
				$('.coupon-item').removeClass('show-detail')
			})
			$(document).on('mouseleave', '.coupon-item', function(e) {
				$('.coupon-item').removeClass('show-detail')
			})

		}

		$(document).on('click', '.coupon-item .close-detail-btn', function() {
			$(this).parents('.coupon-item').removeClass('show-detail')
		})
		first_load = false;
	})
</script>

	Haravan.getParam = function(name, url) {
		if(url == undefined){
			url = location;
		}
		name = name.replace(/[\[]/, '\\[').replace(/[\]]/, '\\]');
		var regex = new RegExp('[\\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)');
		var results = regex.exec(url.search);
		return results === null ? '' : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
	};

<script>
	$('.checkRecover').click(function(e) {
		e.prevevntDefault();
		if ($('input#recover-email').val().indexOf('@') == -1) {
			On_PhoneAuthRecaptchaCallback();
		} else {
			$('#recover-password form').submit();
		}
	})
	function On_PhoneAuthRecaptchaCallback(token) {
		var frm = $('#phone_auth_recaptcha');

		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			url: '/phone_auth/send_verify_code',
			data: frm.serialize(),
			dataType: "json",
			success: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
				if (data && data.token) {
					if ($('#session_info').length > 0) {
						$('#session_info').val(data.token);
						$('#phone_auth_recaptcha').hide();
						$('.otpcode').show();
					}
				}
			},
			error: function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
			}
		});
	}
	$('#otp_submit').click(function() {
		var otpCode = $(this).closest('.otpcode-form').find('#otp_code').val();
		if (otpCode == '') {
			$(this).closest('.otpcode-form').find('.error').html('Quý khách vui lòng nhập chính xác mã OTP được gửi đến số điện thoại của quý khách');
		} else {
			$(this).closest('.otpcode-form').submit();
		}
	})
</script>

<script>
	// Add a leading '0' if the number is less than 10
	function pad(number) {
		return (number < 10 ? '0' : '') + number;
	}
	function parseDateTime(dateTimeStr) {
		const parts = dateTimeStr.split(/ ?- ?/); // Split with or without space around hyphen
		if (parts.length === 2) {  // Date and time provided
			const [day, month, year] = parts[0].split("/");
			const [hours, minutes] = parts[1].split(":");
			return new Date(year, month - 1, day, hours, minutes);
		} else {  // Only date provided
			const [day, month, year] = parts[0].split("/");
			return new Date(year, month - 1, day, 0, 0); // Default time to 00:00
		}
	}

	function countdownInit(type, date,target){
		let countDownDate = parseDateTime(date).getTime();
		let x = setInterval(function() {
			// Get current time in the specified timezone
			let now = new Date().toLocaleString("en-US", { timeZone: "Asia/Ho_Chi_Minh" });
			now = new Date(now).getTime(); 
			let distance = countDownDate - now;
			let days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
			let hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
			let minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
			let seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);
			target.find(".timer.days").text(pad(days));
			target.find(".timer.hours").text(pad(hours));
			target.find(".timer.minutes").text(pad(minutes));
			target.find(".timer.seconds").text(pad(seconds));
			if (distance < 0) {
				clearInterval(x);
				indexCampaignInit()
			}
		}, 1000);
	}
	function indexCampaignInit(target){
		console.log(target)
		const start = target.attr('data-start')
		const end = target.attr('data-end')
		const startTimestamp = parseDateTime(start).getTime(); // Milliseconds
		const endTimestamp = parseDateTime(end).getTime(); // Milliseconds
		let currentTimestamp = new Date().toLocaleString("en-US", { timeZone: "Asia/Ho_Chi_Minh" });
		currentTimestamp = new Date(currentTimestamp).getTime()
		if(currentTimestamp < startTimestamp){
			countdownInit("start", start,target)
			target.find('.countdown-box .title p').text("SẮP MỞ BÁN");
			target.show();
			target.find('.countdown-inventory').remove();
		} 
		else if(currentTimestamp <= endTimestamp){
			countdownInit("end", end,target)
			target.find('.countdown-box .title p').text("ĐẶT NGAY RƯỚC QUÀ TO");
			target.show();
			target.find('.countdown-actions').show();
			target.find('.countdown-inventory').show();
		}
		else{
			target.remove();

		};
	}
	function postToGoogle() {
		const name = $(".campaign-form-name").val();
		const phone = $(".campaign-form-phone").val();
		const data= { 
			"entry.1305318191": name,
			"entry.780519278": phone,
		}
		const url = "https://docs.google.com/forms/u/0/d/e/1FAIpQLSdLkNLImFPsc2qRYovD4cdND2mwrx-J_fLSmh66gG6SKF8Vrw/formResponse?"
		$.ajax({
			url, data,
			type: "POST",
			dataType: "xml",
			success: function(d){}, 
			error: function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
				if (jqXHR.status === 0) { 
					$('#index-campaign-modal').modal('hide');
					swal({
						title: 'Thông báo',
						text: 'Bạn đã đăng ký thành công.',
						icon: 'success',
						showCancelButton: false,
						showConfirmButton: true,
						confirmButtonText: 'Đóng',
						cancelButtonText: 'Không',
					}).then((result) => {
					})
					$("#campaign-contact-form").trigger("reset");
					$("#campaign-contact-form").removeClass('not-submit');
				} else {
					console.error('Error:', errorThrown); 
					$("#campaign-contact-form").removeClass('not-submit');
				}
			}
		});
		return false;
	}
	$(document).ready(function() {
		if($('.campaign-countdown').length > 0){
			$('.campaign-countdown').each(function(i,v){
				indexCampaignInit($(this));
			})
		}
		$(document).on('click', '.btn-popup-form', function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			$('#index-campaign-modal').modal('show')

		})
		const $campaignform = $('#campaign-contact-form')
		$campaignform.on('submit', function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			$campaignform.addClass('not-submit');
			postToGoogle()
		})
		setTimeout(function(){
			$('.product-quantity #quantity').val(1);
		},500)
	})
</script>
